  <script>
      
      $(document).ready(function () {
          
          var abTest = $('.ab-test-sticky-header').text().trim();          
          var keepClosed = false;          
          switch (abTest)
          {
            case "nocase" :
                // do nothing
                break;
            case "caseone" :
                InitCaseOne();
                break;
            case "casetwo" :
                InitCaseTwo();
                break;
            default :
                // do nothing
                break;
          }

          function nocase()
          {
            
          }

          function InitCaseOne()
          {
            HideSideSearchBar()
            ShowCaseOne();
            InitializeStickies();            
            
          }

          function InitCaseTwo()
          { 
            HideSideSearchBar()                       
            ShowCaseTwo();
            InitializeStickies();            
          }

          function HideSideSearchBar()
          {
            $('.ab-test-show-nocase').hide();
          }

          
          function ScrollAndToggle()
          {
              $(window).scroll(function () {                          
                if (!keepClosed)
                {
                      var scrollHeight = $(window).scrollTop();
                      var defaultStickyHeight = 100;
                      if (scrollHeight >= defaultStickyHeight) {
                          //$('#search_bar').next().hide().prev().show();
                          TurnOnSticky();
                      } else {
                          TurnOffSticky();
                          console.log('h');
                      }
                }
              });
          }

          function InitializeStickies()
          {                        
            if (CheckXIconCookie())
            {                
                ScrollAndToggle();
                ClickSearch();
                ClickX();            
            }
          }

          function TurnOnSticky()
          {
            $('.attach-fixed').css({
                position : 'fixed',
                width : '100%',
                zIndex : '10'
            });
            $('.attach-fixed-main-links').css({
                position : 'fixed',
                width : '100%',
                zIndex : '10',
                top : '72px'
            });
            // browse bar
            $('.hook-remove').hide();
            // little spotlights
            $('.hook-remove-background').removeClass('background1');
          }

          function TurnOffSticky()
          {
            // browse bar
            $('.hook-remove').show();
            $('.attach-fixed').css({
                position : 'relative',

            });
            $('.attach-fixed-main-links').css({
                position : 'relative',
                width : '100%',
                zIndex : '10',
                top : 'auto'
            });
            // little spotlights
            $('.hook-remove-background').addClass('background1');
          }

          function ShowCaseOne()
          { 
            keepClosed = true;                     
            $('#ab-test-case-one').show();
            $('.ab-test-hide-on-nocase').css('visibility','visible').show();                 
          }

          function ShowCaseTwo()
          {            
            $('#ab-test-case-two').show();
            $('.ab-test-hide-on-nocase').css('visibility','visible').show();
          }

          function CheckXIconCookie()
          {
            if (typeof($.cookie('close_x')) != 'undefined')
            {
                keepClosed = $.cookie('close_x');
                if (keepClosed === true)
                {
                    return false;
                }            
            }
            return true;                                    
          }

          function ClickX()
          {
              $('.MdBlue').click(function () {
                  $('#search_bar').next().show().prev().hide();
                  keepClosed = true;
                  $.cookie('close_x', true);
              });
          }

          function ClickSearch()
          {
              $('#sticky-search').click(function () {
                  var query = $(this).prev().val();                                 
                  window.location.href = "http://www.entertainmentearth.com/hitlist.asp?searchfield=" + URLencode(query);
              });
          }
         
      });

  </script>
